# VitTrade Compact First-Viewport Density Rollout Report

Generated: 2026-06-20

Scope: whole routed Flutter app, documentation only. This report does not authorize production UI edits by itself; each future screen edit must run GitNexus impact analysis first.

## Executive Summary

- Total real routed pages covered: `414`.
- Redirect aliases excluded from page work: `3`.
- Coverage ledger rows in this report: `414`; route truth mismatches: `0`.
- Screens passing the current visual-density gate after the P2-A implementation batch: `154`.
- Screens requiring tracking/work after the P2-A implementation batch: `260` = `5` fullscreen/tool QA exceptions + `107` P2 rows + `148` P3 rows.
- P2-A batch outcome: all `12` first-batch screens now have focused first-viewport widget coverage; `6` rows moved out of P2, `1` moved to `PASS_MONITOR`, and `6` remain P2 because static line-height/bottom-inset signals still score above threshold despite visible first-viewport evidence.
- Current P0 and P1 regular density backlog is zero; do not create churn in P3/pass rows unless nearby work or QA evidence justifies it.
- Home remains the visual density baseline: compact `VitPageContent`, useful stacked sections, and action/next-section visibility before bottom-nav pressure.
- Fullscreen/tool routes are exceptions: keep tool treatment and prove workspace usage with emulator/widget evidence instead of normal content-page compaction.

### Known Stale Artifacts And Audit Limitations

- `docs/03_DESIGN_SYSTEM/VitTrade-UI-Fullscreen-Density-Home-Standard-Audit.md` is stale for counts: it says 33 flagged routes, while the current `ui_fullscreen_density_audit.dart --check` reports 11 flagged routes plus 403 pass/low-signal rows.
- Some historical tracking-plan rows mention older P3/pass totals; the command outputs in this report are authoritative for this rollout.
- Static source signals cannot prove the actual rendered first viewport. Use widget/emulator evidence for representative route batches, financial confirmations, and fullscreen tools.
- The static visual-density audit can count typography `TextStyle.height` tokens and shared review-section/bottom-inset references as fixed-height pressure. Do not replace readable shared line-height tokens with raw numbers just to reduce the score; document the exception when first-viewport tests pass.
- Shared-component compliance can still be sparse; a screen can pass body/component structure while delaying useful content below the fold.
- Do not compact fullscreen tools with ordinary content-page rules unless evidence shows wasted workspace.


All three checks passed and reported current artifacts.

Post-batch verification from `flutter_app/` after the 12 P2-A edits:

```powershell
dart run tool/visual_density_risk_audit.dart --check
```

Current result: `414` routed screens, `P0=0`, `P1=0`, `P1_TOOL_VISUAL_QA=5`, `P2=107`, `P3=148`, `PASS=154`.

## Priority Order

1. P0 regular density rows: none currently; if reintroduced, stop broad rollout and fix first.
2. P1 regular density rows: none currently; if reintroduced, fix after P0 and before P2 work.
3. `P1_TOOL_VISUAL_QA`: verify tool routes with fullscreen evidence, not normal content compaction.
4. `P2-A next-batch candidate`: first proactive implementation batch.
5. `P2-B medium monitor`: compact when touched or when QA shows a regression.
6. `P2-C standard monitor`: compact when touched or when useful-content visibility is poor.
7. `P3 when-touched monitor`: avoid churn; apply density DoD only when the screen is already being edited.
8. `PASS_MONITOR`: use as reference unless concrete UI evidence says otherwise.

- Prefer shared `VitPageLayout`, `VitPageContent`, `VitCard`, `VitMetricCard`, `VitModuleSectionHeader`, `VitInfoRow`, and `VitHighRiskStatePanel` before local spacing fixes.
- Add or update first-viewport widget assertions with `test/helpers/first_viewport_test_utils.dart` for proactive batches.

## Per-Screen Fix Recipe

Apply this sequence to every non-pass row:

1. Inspect the current layout, source files, and existing focused test.
2. Run GitNexus impact analysis before editing the target page/widget symbol and warn if HIGH or CRITICAL risk appears.
3. Replace relaxed/manual spacing with shared compact density only where it preserves meaning and product safety.
4. Reduce oversized hero/card heights and avoid repeated tall cards before useful content.
5. Move the primary action or next useful section into the first phone viewport, above bottom-nav/sticky-footer pressure.
6. Remove unnecessary `Spacer()` or fixed-height pressure inside cards.
7. Preserve required safety copy, semantics, readable text, touch targets, and Prediction/Open Arena boundaries.
8. Add or update a practical first-viewport widget test where the route has meaningful UI surface coverage.
9. Rerun the focused test, `flutter analyze`, and both density audit checks.

## Definition Of Done

A page is complete only when all of these are true:

- The first viewport shows useful content, not mostly chrome, gaps, hero space, or bottom padding.
- The primary action or next useful section is visible or clearly previewed above the bottom nav/sticky footer.
- No important content is hidden by bottom nav, footer, keyboard, safe area, or sticky CTA clearance.
- Readability, text hierarchy, contrast, semantics, focus order, and 44dp-class touch targets remain safe.
- Financial safety copy remains intact: fees, risk, limits, masking, preview/confirm/receipt, and next steps stay visible where required.
- Prediction Markets and Open Arena remain separate: Prediction can use positions/probability/orders/receipts/P/L; Arena stays points-only.
- Focused tests pass for the touched route or feature.
- `flutter analyze` passes for touched scope before handoff.
- `dart run tool/visual_density_risk_audit.dart --check` improves the score or the exception is documented with evidence.
- `dart run tool/ui_fullscreen_density_audit.dart --check` stays current.

## Command Set For The Next Execution AI

Run from `flutter_app/` before selecting or editing screens:

```powershell
dart run tool/route_coverage_audit.dart --check
dart run tool/visual_density_risk_audit.dart --check
dart run tool/ui_fullscreen_density_audit.dart --check
```

Before each screen edit, run GitNexus impact on the target symbol. After each focused implementation batch, run:

```powershell
flutter test test/features/<feature>/<page_test>.dart --reporter=compact
flutter analyze
dart run tool/visual_density_risk_audit.dart --check
dart run tool/ui_fullscreen_density_audit.dart --check
```

For fullscreen tools, add emulator/widget screenshot evidence and do not force normal content-page compaction without visual proof.
